Motifs are smooth and subtle, there is a mix of shapes and textures- with no strict adherence to a particular theme  There is a good amount of furniture in most rooms but no clutter or unnecessary decor, the furniture layouts are also very â€œnormalâ€, the types of layouts you will find in many middle income homes- just with larger furniture and bigger rooms. There is also no unrealistic or uncomfortable furniture (like square plastic chairs or pure white fabric furniture)  The lighting color mimics natural light, it is soft and allows for shadows, the lighting is really consistent throughout the house  There are meaningful mementos rather than â€œjust for showâ€ decor - and the house is lived in!
